This JSON object contains a single property 'data' which is an object that contains a single property 'TF\_QUESTIONNAIRES'. 'TF\_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. Each question in the 'TF\_QUESTIONS' array has a 'CODE', 'NAME', 'TYPE\_ID', 'DISPLAY\_ORDER' and an array of answers 'TF\_ANSWERS'. The 'CODE' and 'NAME' are used to identify the question and 'TYPE\_ID' is used to determine the type of question. 'DISPLAY\_ORDER' is used to determine the order in which the questions should be displayed. The 'TF\_ANSWERS' array contains the different possible answers for the question. The 'ANSWER' property is used to determine the text of the answer and in some cases, other properties like 'color', 'intensity', 'reasons', 'impact', 'agree', 'affected', 'cause' and 'improve' are used to capture additional information about the answer.

Each question has a unique code, name, type (1 for choosing one answer from a list, 3 for rating something, and 4 for acquiring feedback), display order, and possible answers. The questionnaire's code is "HEALTH\_SAFETY\_MEASURES", and its name is "Health and Safety Measures Questionnaire". The five questions are about awareness of basic hygiene practices among employees, PPE supply chain satisfaction, training effectiveness on health and safety, availability and accessibility of materials, and communication regarding health & safety protocol.

     - Question number: 7

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.
Firstly, the user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Then, the user will ask to convert it into a specified format.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. 

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Culture with 7 questions

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a set of seven engagingquestions about workplace culture:
1) If you were asked to describe our company's current work environment in three words, what would they be? Please share thosewords and explain whyyou chose them. *^(3excitementpointsforthisquestion)* 2 )How often do we say "please"and 'thank-younessary", or is it more of a commanddriven culture?"Please provide youranswer using thefollowing scale:1 (never),50% - not really,76.348*percent(yesbutnotideal) and 92+ percent = always.*^
[Answer]("please"and "thank-you": Always; Commanddriven culture : Never)* ^ **Strongly agree that we should be saying please & thank you more often** \*\*.\*3.
